                                ', Founded in April 2014 in Silicon Valley, Droom is India\u2019s first online marketplace to buy and sell new and used automobiles and automobile services. Droom has taken a completely innovative and disruptive approach to build trust and pricing advantages for buyers.', 
                                ', The current experience of buying and selling an automobile is completely broken, antiquated and full of pitfalls. Droom offers a truly 21st century experience in buying and selling automobiles. With its technology driven marketplace approach, Droom enables transactions between buyers and sellers by bringing transparency, building trust, and mitigating information asymmetry. Droom is a mobile first marketplace with a presence on three platforms i.e. Android, iOS and Desktop.', 
                                ', Droom is among the fastest growing consumer Internet companies in India with 83K+ B2C sellers, 25K+ products, 114K+ listings,  Rs 6,406Cr+ in listed GMV, 3.28Mil+ FB Community members (highest for any automobile community in India) and 3.9Mil+ downloads for mobile apps. ', 
                                ', Droom is funded by some of the leading global venture investors and has a very strong and proven founding team with 75 years of combined experience in technology, Internet, E-Commerce and FMCG including 35 years in Silicon Valley.  Droom has a team of 218 in its offices in Gurgaon (India) and Silicon Valley (USA).',

                    di.find(".u-di").html("DID: <strong>" + cook.di + "</strong>");
                    else if (typeof cook.ui !== 'undefined' && cook.ui != '' && cook.ui != null)
                    di.find(".u-di").html("UID: <strong>" + cook.ui + "</strong>");
                    if (typeof cook.ln !== 'undefined' && cook.ln != '' && cook.ln != null)
                    ln = cook.ln;
                    di.find(".u-fn1").html("Hi&nbsp;" + cook.fn);
                    di.find(".u-fn2").html("Hi&nbsp;" + cook.fn);
                    di.find(".u-fun").html(fn + "&nbsp;" + ln);
                    if (typeof cook.pp !== 'undefined' && cook.pp != '' && cook.pp != null)
                    di.find(".u-pp").html("<img src='" + cook.pp + "' alt='" + fn + "&nbsp;" + ln + "'>")
                    else
                    di.find(".u-pp").html("<img src='http://droom.in/themes/frontend/images/loginProfile.png' alt='User'>")
                    if (typeof cook.em !== 'undefined' && cook.em != '' && cook.em != null) {
            di.find(".u-e").html(cook.em);
            }
            if (typeof cook.pr !== 'undefined' && cook.pr == 1)
                    di.find(".u-pr").html("My Storemanager");
                    else
                    di.find(".u-pr").html("My Account");
                    di.find(".before-login").addClass("hide");
                    di.find(".after-login").removeClass("hide");
            }
            }

            function show_loggedout_data(){
            var di = $(document).find("div.hd_usr_det");
                    di.find(".after-login").addClass("hide");
                    di.find(".before-login").removeClass("hide");
                    di.find(".u-fn1").html("");
                    di.find(".u-fn2").html("");
                    di.find(".u-fun").html("");
                    di.find(".u-pp").html("");
                    di.find(".u-e").html("");
                    di.find(".u-pr").html("");
                    $.ajax({
                    url: "/del_cookie",
                            type: 'get',
                            data:{},
                            success: function (data) {
                            //console.log(data);
                            }
                    });
            }

            //-----------------------------------------------------
            function getCookie(cname) {
            var name = cname + "=";
                    var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
                    for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
            var c = ca[i];
                    while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
            c = c.substring(1);
            }
            if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
            return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
            }
            }
            return "";
            }

                    // Load Popup on page Load
                    $(document).ready(function () {

            var cookie = getCookie('drm_hm_pop');
                    if (cookie != 1) {
            $('#load-popup').modal('show');
                    ga('set', 'nonInteraction', true);
                    ga('send', 'event', {
                    eventCategory: 'Pop up for email', eventAction: 'Load', eventLabel: 'Click Submit', eventValue: 1
                    });
            }
            });
                    function setCookie(cname, cvalue, exdays) {
                    var d = new Date();
                            d.setTime(d.getTime() + (exdays * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
                            var expires = "expires=" + d.toUTCString();
                            document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + "; " + expires + ";domain=.droom.in;path=/";
                    }
            function getCookie(cname) {
            var name = cname + "=";
                    var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
                    for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
            var c = ca[i];
                    while (c.charAt(0) == ' ')
                    c = c.substring(1);
                    if (c.indexOf(name) == 0)
                    return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
            }
            return "";
            }
            function deleteCookie(name) {
            setCookie(name, "", - 1);
            }

            //select the location
            function getParameterByName(name) {
            name = name.replace(/[\[]/, "\\[").replace(/[\]]/, "\\]");
                    var regex = new RegExp("[\\?&]" + name + "=([^&#]*)"),
                    results = regex.exec(window.location.search);
                    return results === null ? "" : decodeURIComponent(results[1].replace(/\+/g, " "));
            }

            var location = getParameterByName('user_location') ? getParameterByName('user_location') : getCookie('user_location');
                    if (location) {
            $("#location-name").text(location);
            }

            $('.insert-loc').on('click', 'li', function(){
            var loc = $(this).find('a').html();
                    loc = $.trim(loc);
                    if (loc){
            if (loc == 'All Cities'){
            setCookie("user_location", '', 0.000000000000001);
            } else{
            setCookie('user_location', loc, 10);
            }
            }

                    $('#location-search, #location-search-mob').click(function () {

            var req = "",
                    base_url = "http://droom.in/v2/popular_cities-search";
                    if ($(this).closest('div[class^="dropdown"]').hasClass('open') == false){
            $.ajax({
            url: base_url,
                    type: 'get',
                    dataType: 'JSON',
                    data: {require: 1},
                    success: function (data) {

                    if (data['code_success'] == 1) {

                    $('.insert-loc').find('li').remove();
                                                        var url = 'search?status=active';
                                                        $('.insert-loc').html('<li><a href="/' + url + '&location=All%20Cities" style="color: #cc0000;font-weight: bold; padding-left: 10px;">All Cities</a></li>');
                            jQuery.each(data['cities'], function (i, val) {


                            if (val == 'Ahmedabad'){


                            $('.insert-loc').append('<li style="padding-left:10px"><strong>Popular Cities</strong></li>');
                            }

                            if (val == 'Achalpur'){


                            $('.insert-loc').append('<li style="padding-left:10px"><strong>Other Cities</strong></li>');
                            }
                            if (req == val) {
                                                                $('.insert-loc').append("<li class='nav-active'><a href='/" + url + "&city=" + val + "'>" + val + "</a></li>");
                                                                } else {
                                                                $('.insert-loc').append("<li><a href='/" + url + "&city=" + val + "' > " + val + " </a></li>");
                                                                }

                            });
                    }
                    }
            });

                            function errorSuccessMessage(message, type, time){
                            $('.errorSuccessModal').fadeIn();
                                    $('.errorSuccessModal').removeClass('bg-danger');
                                    $('.errorSuccessModal').removeClass('bg-success');
                                    if (type == 'message'){
                            $('.errorSuccessModal').addClass('bg-success');

                            }

$(document).ready(function(){
    
    $(".tabbing ul li:first a").addClass("selectedtab");
    $(".tabbing-content:eq(0)").show();
    $(".tabbing ul li a").click(function(){
        var tabid = $(this).attr('rel');
        $(".tabbing ul li a").removeClass('selectedtab');
        $(this).addClass('selectedtab');
        $('.tabbing-content').hide();
        $(tabid).slideToggle('slow');
        return false;
    });
    $('.help-block').hide();
});
        
$('#apply_btn').click(function() {
    $('.form-group').removeClass('has-error');
    $('.help-block').hide();
    // Validations
    if ($('#first_name').val() == "") {
        $('#first_name').closest('.form-group').addClass('has-error');
        $('#first_name').siblings('.help-block').show();
        $('#first_name').focus();
        return false;
    }

    if ($('#last_name').val() == "") {
        $('#last_name').closest('.form-group').addClass('has-error');
        $('#last_name').siblings('.help-block').show();
        $('#last_name').focus();
        return false;
    }

    if ($('#email').val() == "") {
        $('#email').closest('.form-group').addClass('has-error');
        $('#email').siblings('.help-block').show();
        $('#email').focus();
        return false;
    } else {
        var candidate_email = $('#email').val();
        if (/(.+)@(.+){2,}\.(.+){2,}/.test(candidate_email)){
            // valid email
        } else {
            $('#email').closest('.form-group').addClass('has-error');
            $('#email').siblings('.help-block').show();
            $('#email').focus();
            return false;
        }
    }
    
    if ($('#phone').val() == "") {
        $('#phone').closest('.form-group').addClass('has-error');
        $('#phone').siblings('.help-block').show();
        $('#phone').focus();
        return false;
    } else {
        var mobile_no = $('#phone').val();
        if (mobile_no.length != 10 || mobile_no < 7000000000) {
            $('#phone').closest('.form-group').addClass('has-error');
            $('#phone').siblings('.help-block').show();
            $('#phone').focus();
            return false;
        }
    }

    if ($('#career_role option:selected').val() == "") {
        $('#career_role').closest('.form-group').addClass('has-error');
        $('#career_role').siblings('.help-block').show();
        $('#career_role').focus();
        return false;
    }
    
    if ($('#career_role option:selected').val() == "") {
        $('#career_role').closest('.form-group').addClass('has-error');
        $('#career_role').siblings('.help-block').show();
        $('#career_role').focus();
        return false;
    } 

    if ($('#career_role option:selected').val() == "") {
        $('#career_role').closest('.form-group').addClass('has-error');
        $('#career_role').siblings('.help-block').show();
        $('#career_role').focus();
        return false; 
    } else {
        var career_position = $('#career_role option:selected').text(); 
        $("#career_position").val(career_position); 
    } 

    if ($('#input-resume').val() == "") {
        $('#input-resume').closest('.form-group').addClass('has-error');
        $('#input-resume').closest('.form-group').find('.help-block').show();
        $('#input-resume').focus();
        return false; 
    } 
});

$('.item-department').children('[data-toggle="collapse"]').click(function(){
    $(this).parent('.item-department').toggleClass('focused') 
    $(this).parent('.item-department').siblings('.item-department').removeClass('focused') 
    var el_id = $(this).attr('aria-controls'); 
    $('#' + el_id).siblings('.collapse').removeClass('in'); 
}); 

$('.btn-view-position').click(function(){
    $(this).text(function(i, text){
        return text === "Hide Positions" ? "View Positions" : "Hide Positions"; 
    }); 
    $(this).closest('.item-department').siblings().find('.btn-view-position').text('View Positions'); 
});

    $(this).text(function(i, text){
        return text === "Hide Details" ? "View Details" : "Hide Details"; 
    }); 
    $(this).closest('.panel-default').siblings().find('[data-toggle="collapse"]').text('View Details');
});

            function show_login_data(cook){
            var di = $(document).find("div.hd_usr_det");
                    if (cook != '' && typeof di !== 'undefined' && di.length) {
            var fn = ''; var ln = '';
                    if (typeof cook.fn !== 'undefined' && cook.fn != '' && cook.fn != null)
                    fn = cook.fn;
                    if (typeof cook.di !== 'undefined' && cook.di != '' && cook.di != null)
                    di.find(".u-di").html("DID: <strong>" + cook.di + "</strong>");
                    else if (typeof cook.ui !== 'undefined' && cook.ui != '' && cook.ui != null)
                    di.find(".u-di").html("UID: <strong>" + cook.ui + "</strong>");
                    if (typeof cook.ln !== 'undefined' && cook.ln != '' && cook.ln != null)
                    ln = cook.ln;
                    di.find(".u-fn1").html("Hi&nbsp;" + cook.fn);
                    di.find(".u-fn2").html("Hi&nbsp;" + cook.fn);
                    di.find(".u-fun").html(fn + "&nbsp;" + ln);
                    if (typeof cook.pp !== 'undefined' && cook.pp != '' && cook.pp != null)
                    di.find(".u-pp").html("<img src='" + cook.pp + "' alt='" + fn + "&nbsp;" + ln + "'>")
                    else
                    di.find(".u-pp").html("<img src='http://droom.in/themes/frontend/images/loginProfile.png' alt='User'>")
                    if (typeof cook.em !== 'undefined' && cook.em != '' && cook.em != null) {
            di.find(".u-e").html(cook.em);
            }
            if (typeof cook.pr !== 'undefined' && cook.pr == 1)
                    di.find(".u-pr").html("My Storemanager");
                    else
                    di.find(".u-pr").html("My Account");
                    di.find(".before-login").addClass("hide");
                    di.find(".after-login").removeClass("hide");
            }
            }

            function show_loggedout_data(){
            var di = $(document).find("div.hd_usr_det");
                    di.find(".after-login").addClass("hide");
                    di.find(".before-login").removeClass("hide");

            //-----------------------------------------------------
            function getCookie(cname) {
            var name = cname + "=";
                    var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
                    for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
            var c = ca[i];
                    while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
            c = c.substring(1);
            }
            if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
            return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
            }
            }
            return "";
            }

                    // Load Popup on page Load
                    $(document).ready(function () {

                    if (cookie != 1) {
            $('#load-popup').modal('show');
                    ga('set', 'nonInteraction', true);

                    function setCookie(cname, cvalue, exdays) {
                    var d = new Date();
                            d.setTime(d.getTime() + (exdays * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
                            var expires = "expires=" + d.toUTCString();
                            document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + "; " + expires + ";domain=.droom.in;path=/";
                    }
            function getCookie(cname) {
            var name = cname + "=";
                    var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
                    for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
            var c = ca[i];
                    while (c.charAt(0) == ' ')
                    c = c.substring(1);
                    if (c.indexOf(name) == 0)
                    return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
            }
            return "";
            }
            function deleteCookie(name) {
            setCookie(name, "", - 1);
            }

                    $(window).load(function () {

            //select the location
            function getParameterByName(name) {
            name = name.replace(/[\[]/, "\\[").replace(/[\]]/, "\\]");
                    var regex = new RegExp("[\\?&]" + name + "=([^&#]*)"),
                    results = regex.exec(window.location.search);
                    return results === null ? "" : decodeURIComponent(results[1].replace(/\+/g, " "));
            }

            var location = getParameterByName('user_location') ? getParameterByName('user_location') : getCookie('user_location');
                    if (location) {
            $("#location-name").text(location);
            }

            $('.insert-loc').on('click', 'li', function(){

                    if (loc){
            if (loc == 'All Cities'){
            setCookie("user_location", '', 0.000000000000001);
            } else{
            setCookie('user_location', loc, 10);
            }
            }

                            function errorSuccessMessage(message, type, time){
                            $('.errorSuccessModal').fadeIn();
                                    $('.errorSuccessModal').removeClass('bg-danger');
                                    $('.errorSuccessModal').removeClass('bg-success');
                                    if (type == 'message'){
                            $('.errorSuccessModal').addClass('bg-success');
                            } else{
                            $('.errorSuccessModal').addClass('bg-danger');
                            }
                            $('#pop-custom').html(message);
                                    setTimeout(function(){ $('.errorSuccessModal').fadeOut() }, time);
                            }

                    $('.errorSuccessModal span').click(function(){
                    $(this).parent().fadeOut();
                    })

$(document).ready(function(){
    
    $(".tabbing ul li:first a").addClass("selectedtab");
    $(".tabbing-content:eq(0)").show();
    $(".tabbing ul li a").click(function(){
        var tabid = $(this).attr('rel');
        $(".tabbing ul li a").removeClass('selectedtab');
        $(this).addClass('selectedtab');
        $('.tabbing-content').hide();
        $(tabid).slideToggle('slow');
        return false;
    });
    $('.help-block').hide();
});
        
$('#apply_btn').click(function() {
    $('.form-group').removeClass('has-error');
    $('.help-block').hide();
    // Validations
    if ($('#first_name').val() == "") {
        $('#first_name').closest('.form-group').addClass('has-error');
        $('#first_name').siblings('.help-block').show();
        $('#first_name').focus();
        return false;
    }

    if ($('#last_name').val() == "") {
        $('#last_name').closest('.form-group').addClass('has-error');
        $('#last_name').siblings('.help-block').show();
        $('#last_name').focus();
        return false;
    }

    if ($('#email').val() == "") {
        $('#email').closest('.form-group').addClass('has-error');
        $('#email').siblings('.help-block').show();
        $('#email').focus();
        return false;
    } else {
        var candidate_email = $('#email').val();
        if (/(.+)@(.+){2,}\.(.+){2,}/.test(candidate_email)){
            // valid email
        } else {
            $('#email').closest('.form-group').addClass('has-error');
            $('#email').siblings('.help-block').show();
            $('#email').focus();
            return false;
        }
    }
    
    if ($('#phone').val() == "") {
        $('#phone').closest('.form-group').addClass('has-error');
        $('#phone').siblings('.help-block').show();
        $('#phone').focus();
        return false;
    } else {
        var mobile_no = $('#phone').val();
        if (mobile_no.length != 10 || mobile_no < 7000000000) {
            $('#phone').closest('.form-group').addClass('has-error');
            $('#phone').siblings('.help-block').show();
            $('#phone').focus();
            return false;
        }
    }

    if ($('#career_role option:selected').val() == "") {
        $('#career_role').closest('.form-group').addClass('has-error');
        $('#career_role').siblings('.help-block').show();
        $('#career_role').focus();
        return false;
    }
    
    if ($('#career_role option:selected').val() == "") {
        $('#career_role').closest('.form-group').addClass('has-error');
        $('#career_role').siblings('.help-block').show();
        $('#career_role').focus();
        return false;
    } 

    if ($('#career_role option:selected').val() == "") {
        $('#career_role').closest('.form-group').addClass('has-error');
        $('#career_role').siblings('.help-block').show();
        $('#career_role').focus();
        return false; 
    } else {
        var career_position = $('#career_role option:selected').text(); 
        $("#career_position").val(career_position); 
    } 

    if ($('#input-resume').val() == "") {
        $('#input-resume').closest('.form-group').addClass('has-error');
        $('#input-resume').closest('.form-group').find('.help-block').show();
        $('#input-resume').focus();
        return false; 
    } 
});
        

// Career Departments Collapse | Ajit
$('.item-department').children('[data-toggle="collapse"]').click(function(){
    $(this).parent('.item-department').toggleClass('focused') 
    $(this).parent('.item-department').siblings('.item-department').removeClass('focused') 
    var el_id = $(this).attr('aria-controls'); 
    $('#' + el_id).siblings('.collapse').removeClass('in'); 
}); 

$('.btn-view-position').click(function(){
    $(this).text(function(i, text){
        return text === "Hide Positions" ? "View Positions" : "Hide Positions"; 
    }); 
    $(this).closest('.item-department').siblings().find('.btn-view-position').text('View Positions'); 
}); 

$('.positions-accordion').find('.btn-link').click(function(){
    $(this).text(function(i, text){
        return text === "Hide Details" ? "View Details" : "Hide Details"; 
    }); 
    $(this).closest('.panel-default').siblings().find('[data-toggle="collapse"]').text('View Details');
});
